plane-crazy 2021-08-19 16:04:51 There are methods of detonating the explosives. One of which includes upon contact. As the name states the tnt will explode upon contact occasionally with conditions such as minimum impact speed requires to activate such action or arm on key requires the arming of the explosives through a button before it can activate its function. Ignore self is simply another condition of this. The explosive will explode whenever it meets the conditions stated before but now its simply the condition of where it explodes. If it meets the condition, but these conditions are met __while hitting__ your blocks the explosive __will not__ activate but if the conditions are met __while not hitting__ your blocks the explosives __will__ activate.

plane-crazy 2021-09-04 02:42:14 So motorlocking, motorlocking is a style of building enabled by the lock feature on the motors. This feature allows motors to move a connected block down by half a block. Chaining multiple of them allows them to no clip an entire section into another section creating a good looking piece. You can motorlock glass cylinders into your canopy section which will create a good looking canopy but there is another motorlocking you can do. Which is angled motorlocking, this allows you pre-set an angle of a section relative to the section it is about to get no-clipped into. This also allows for good looking builds in this case motor lock another cylinder angled down relative to the first canopy and move them both into the canopy area. Though this may be finicky due to relative angles and edge alignments.

plane-crazy 2022-03-14 21:54:27 It's a combination of angle locking and motor locking. Each piece is rotated sufficiently that there is no gap is made, you can do this with trigonometry or a software design tool, then repeat until a full rotation is made. Then each piece is motor locked into each other to form the rounded front. There is a bit of overlap as a result of its inward curved nature but it is mostly round. Though this is very oversimplified in reality it is easier said than done lol
